 aparaadh ko sugam banane ke aashay se yaa sambhawatah uske bare main jaanate hue bhi aise aparaadh kii pariklpana karnaa yaa avaidh rup se swechha purvak aise aparaadh ko chhipaana yaa aparaadh karne ke tareeke kaa varnan karnaa aadi bhartiya dand samhita kii dhara 120 ke tahat hi aata he
 If such a crime is committed to the guilty, then the convict can be sentenced to imprisonment for any one term
 sajaa kii avadhi ek chauthai tak badhaai ja sakati he
 Also, the guilty can be punished with economic punishment or both
 lekin yadi aparaadh nahin hota he, tab bhi doshi ko kisi ek avadhi ke liye karawas kii sajaa ho sakati he
 Or it can be fined or both
 yah aparaadh samjhauta karne yogya nahin he
 Section 376 of IPC (rape of woman) The accused of raping any woman is prosecuted under Section 376 of IPC
 koi purush kisi mahila ke saath uski ichha ke viruddh shaareerik sambandh banaata he, to use balaatkaar kehete hai
 Whether or not the sexual intercourse is completed for any reason, but by law it will be called rape
 doshi ko sajaapraadh siddh ho jane par doshi ko nunatam 7 saal or adhiktam 10 saal kii kadi sajaa die jane kaa praavdhaan he
 In many rare cases, the convict can also be sentenced to life imprisonment
 iske alaava aarthik jurmaana lagaaya ja saktaa he
 If a person has raped his wife, and is not less than twelve years of age, the convict can be sentenced to up to two years if proven guilty
 yaa us par jurmaana bhi lagaaya ja saktaa he
 In many cases courts can shorten the period of sentence for sufficient and special reasons
 balaatkaar ke samay alag-alag halaat or shrenee ke hisaab se ise dhara 375, 376, 376k, 376kha, 376ga, 376gha ke rup main vibhajit kiya gaya he
 Posco Act (minor or sexual exploitation of children) The word poxo comes from English
 iskaa purnakalik matlab hota he protection aaf children fram sexual afences act 2012 yani langik utpeedan se bacchon ke sangrakshan kaa adhinium 2012
 Action is taken in cases of sexual offenses and molestation occurring with minor children under this Act
 yah act bacchon ko sexual herracement, sexual asolt or pornography jaise gambhir aparaadhon se suraksha pradaan karata he
 Under this law enacted in the year 2012, different punishment has been fixed for different crime
 jiskaa kadai se paalan kiya janaa bhi sunishchit kiya gaya he
 The guilty are covered under Section 4 of the Sessions Act in cases where the child has been raped or maltreated
 isamen saat saal sajaa se lekar umrakaid or arthdand bhi lagaaya ja saktaa he
 Cases under Section 6 of the Poxo Act are brought in which children have been severely hurt after rape or misdemeanor
 isamen das saal se lekar umrakaid tak kii sajaa ho sakati he or saath hi jurmaana bhi lagaaya ja saktaa he
 Similarly, cases are registered under Sections 7 and 8 of the Poxo Act in which children are attacked with the genitals
 iske dhara ke aropiyon par dosha siddh ho jane par paanch se saat saal tak kii sajaa or jurmaana ho saktaa he
 Section 363 (kidnapping) of IPC If a person kidnaps a person residing in India or under the protection of a legal guardian, it is an offense under Section 363 of the Indian Penal Code
 aise main doshi qaraar die gaye vyakti ko kisi ek avadhi ke liye karawas kii sajaa ho sakati he
 Which can be extended up to seven years, and can also be fined
 yah ek jamaanti, sangyeya aparaadh he
 The cases registered under this section are heard by first-class magistrates
 yah aparaadh samjhauta karne yogya nahin he
 Section 366 of IPC (coercing, abetting sexual exploitation) if a man compels a woman to marry against the will of a woman, or illegally seduces or compels a woman to have intercourse
 to yah aparaadh bhartiya dand samhita kii dhara 366 ke tahat aata he
 If found guilty, there is a provision for strict action against that person
 doshi ko sajaaaise maamle main doshi to adhiktam 10 varsh ke liye karawas kii sajaa ho sakati he
 At the same time economic punishment can be imposed on the guilty
 yah ek gaiyr-jamaanti sangyeya aparaadh kii shrenee main aata he

 yah aparaadh samjhauta karne yogya nahin he
